***всколыхнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:всколыхнуть.html>всколыхну́ть</a> (26350)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:всколыхнуть.html>всколыхну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vskolyxnútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">всколы́хивать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to rock, to shake, to stir</li>
<li>to stir up, to rouse</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вс-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vs-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кормить.html>корми́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kormítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вскормить.html>вскорми́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vskormítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">вска́рмливать</b>)

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">folk  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to raise, to educate (a child, etc.)</li></ol>

***вскормленный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вскормленный.html>вско́рмленный</a> (26506)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вскормленный.html>вско́рмленный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vskórmlennyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past passive perfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вскормить.html>вскорми́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vskormítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***вскочить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вскочить.html>вскочи́ть</a> (1403)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невдомек.html>в-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-скочи́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-skočítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вскочить.html>вскочи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vskočítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вскакивать.html>вска́кивать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>(unexpectedly) to jump (up, onto, out of), to leap (on, into, onto), to get up quickly
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вскочить.html>вскочи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>ноги</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vskočítʹ</b> ná nogi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to leap / spring to one's feet</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вскочить.html>вскочи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:постель.html>посте́ли</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vskočítʹ</b> s postéli</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to jump out of bed</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to rise, to swell (up), to come up (<i>e.g. a pimple on the face, a bump on the head</i>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:вскочить.html>вскочи́л</a></b> пры́щик <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нос.html>носу́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u menjá <b>vskočíl</b> prýščik na nosú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I've got a pimple on my nose (suddenly)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вскрик.html>вскрик</a> (15058)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вскрик.html>вскрик</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vskrik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вскрик.html>вскри́ка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вскрик.html>вскри́ки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вскрик.html>вскри́ков</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>shriek, cry</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***вскрывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вскрывать.html>вскрыва́ть</a> (11570)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вскрыть.html>вскрыть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vskrytʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вскрывать.html>вскрыва́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vskryvátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вскрыть.html>вскрыть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to open, to unseal
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вскрывать.html>вскрыва́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:письмо.html>письмо́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vskryvátʹ pisʹmó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to open a letter, to tear a letter open</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to reveal, to bring to light, to disclose, to uncover, to expose
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вскрывать.html>вскрыва́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:недостаток.html>недоста́тки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vskryvátʹ nedostátki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to expose shortcomings, to lay bare shortcomings</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to dissect, to make a postmortem, to perform an autopsy on</li>
<li>to burst, to cut, to open, to lance
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вскрывать.html>вскрыва́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нарыв.html>нары́в</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vskryvátʹ narýv</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to cut an abscess</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вскрыть.html>вскрыть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vskrytʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тие</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-tije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вскрытие.html>вскры́тие</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vskrýtije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вскрытие.html>вскры́тия</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вскрытие.html>вскры́тия</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вскрытие.html>вскры́тий</a></b>)

***вскрыть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вскрыть.html>вскрыть</a> (6461)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вс-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vs-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крыть.html>крыть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krytʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вскрыть.html>вскрыть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vskrytʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вскрывать.html>вскрыва́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to open, to unseal
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вскрыть.html>вскрыть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:письмо.html>письмо́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vskrytʹ</b> pisʹmó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to open a letter, to tear a letter open</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to reveal, to bring to light, to disclose, to uncover, to expose
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вскрыть.html>вскрыть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:недостаток.html>недоста́тки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vskrytʹ</b> nedostátki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to expose shortcomings, to lay bare shortcomings</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to dissect, to  make a postmortem, to perform an autopsy on</li>
<li>to burst, to cut, to open, to lance
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вскрыть.html>вскрыть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:нарыв.html>нары́в</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vskrytʹ</b> narýv</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to cut an abscess</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***вслед.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вслед.html>вслед</a> (1290)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вслед.html>вслед</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vsled</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>after, right after, behind, following
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вслед.html>Вслед</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:первый.html>пе́рвой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:колонна.html>коло́нной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:выступить.html>вы́ступила</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:второй.html>втора́я</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Vsled</b> za pérvoj kolónnoj výstupila vtorája</i> ― <span class="e-translation">After the first column came the second.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вслед.html>вслед</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vsled</span>) (+ dative, or <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">za</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> with instrumental)
</p>
<ol><li>after, behind, following
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смотреть.html>смотре́л</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:вслед.html>вслед</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:поезд.html>по́езду</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Smotrél <b>vsled</b> pójezdu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He gazed after the train.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вслед.html>Вслед</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:раздаться.html>разда́ли́сь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:угроза.html>угро́зы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Vsled</b> jemú razdálísʹ ugrózy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Behind him were heard threats.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
